[1b1] / / namo buddhāya /

Vin_1.2 / sarvasmin* sannipatite saṃghe kṛtedaṃ veṣaṃ nipatya pragṛhītāñjalim utkuṭusthaṃ vṛddhāntaṃ yācivantaṃ trir jñapticaturthena karmaṇā saha pravrajyopasaṃpadāv upanayeyur iti purākalpaḥ /
Vin_1.3 / niśritasya kañcid bhikṣuṃ tatropādhyāyatayā pravrajyopasampadau /

Vin_1.104 / nānārādhitacittam utsṛjya śākyam āgneyañ ca jaṭilaṃ tīrthyaṃ pravrajayeyur upasaṃpādayeyur vā kṛte tattīrthyānārādhitāditīrthyānta[ra]varjam* /

**(Vin_1,3) kṣudrakādigatam
Vin_1.146 // kṛdrājabhaṭaḥ /
Vin_1.147 / ananujñātaṃ rājñā 'dūradeśakaṃ /
Vin_1.148 / [3a5] kṛnarodhvajavadhakaḥ /
Vin_1.149 / na rathakāracaṇḍālapukkasatadvidhān* pravrājayet* /
Vin_1.150 / nidarśanaṃ hastachinnādayaḥ /
/ hāridrakeśā harikeśā haritakeśās tathaiva ca /
/ avadātakeśāś ca ye narā nāgakeśā akeśakā /
/ ghāṭāśirā badraśirā atisthūlāś cipāṭakāḥ /
/ kharasūkaraśīrṣāś ca dviśīrṣā apy aśīrṣakāḥ /
/ hastikarṇā aśvakarṇā gaṇa[3a6]margaṭakarṇakāḥ /
/ kharasūkarakarṇāś ca ekakarṇā akarṇakāḥ /
/ lohitākṣā tivadrākṣāś cullākṣātipiṅgalāḥ /
/ kācākṣā budbudakṣāś ca ekākṣāpy anākṣakāḥ /
/ hastināsāśvanāsā goṇamargaṭanāsakāḥ /
/ kharasūkaranāsāś ca ekanāsā [a]nāsakāḥ /
/ hastijoḍā aśvajoḍā goṇamargaṭajoḍakāḥ /
/ kharasūka[3b1]rajoḍāś ca ekajoḍā ajoḍakāḥ /
/ hastidantāśvadantā goṇamargaṭadantakāḥ /
/ kharasūkaradantāś ca ekadantā adantakāḥ /
/ atigrīvā agrīvāś ca skandhākṣā api kubjakāḥ /
/ lāṃgulachinnā vātāṃḍā ekāṇḍāpy anaṇḍakāḥ /
/ atidīrghātihrasvāś ca kriśāś cātikilāsinaḥ /
/ caturbhiś ca chavivarṇaiḥ khelā vikaṭakās tathā /
/ evaṃvidhā[3b2]nam api taṃ pratikṣepaṃ pradhārayet* /

Vin_2.359 / sthūlakṛtvaṃ svalakṣaṇagrāhakasya kleśaviskambhinaḥ śamathanimittasya /

2,4 prāyaścittikam /
**(Vin_2,4,1) mṛṣāvāde /
Vin_2.938 / saṃjñāya saṃghasannidhāv adharmasya dharmato dharmasya cādharmataḥ paridīpanaṃ sthūlātyayaḥ /
Vin_2.939 / kaccit sthā [a]tra pariśuddhā ityā[18b1]tṛtīyapariprasnāt poṣadhe śuddhasaṃjñasya tūṣṇīm bhāvenātināmanāyā duṣkṛtam /

*Vin_4. pravāraṇavastu /
**(Vin_4,1) pravāraṇāvidhiḥ /
Vin_4.1 / na maunaṃ samādadīta /
Vin_4.2 / śuddhi[43b2]m uktyor anena pratyavagatau sthūlātyayaḥ /
Vin_4.3 / dṛṣṭasrutapariśaṅkābhiḥ varṣoṣitaḥ saṃgha pravārayet* /
Vin_4.4 / paścime hni varṣāṇāṃ /
Vin_4.5 / gocarā rocayeyuḥ /
Vin_4.6 / yataḥ prabhṛti kelāyanam iyatbhiḥ divasaiḥ saṃghasya pravāraṇā bhaviṣyati yuṣmākam ārocitam bhavatv iti /
Vin_4.7 / vihārasya maṇḍanam* /
Vin_4.8 / kūṭāgārāṇāṃ bandhanam* /
Vin_4.9 / rāhānāṃ ci[43b3]traṇaṃ stūpānāṃ moccanamolanaṃ ca /
Vin_4.10 / siddhāsanasya maṇḍanam* /
Vin_4.11 / adya sarvarātrikaṃ dharmaśravaṇaṃ bhaviṣyati tatra yuṣmābhiḥ sāmagrī deyeti gocarārocya sūtravinayamātrakadharair adhiṣṭacaturdaśyāṃ sarvarātrikadharmaśravaṇadāpanam* /
Vin_4.12 / parasyāntaiḥ prākkarmato dhamyayā viniścayakathayā rātrer atināmanam* /
Vin_4.13 / prāgaruṇasaṃ[43b4]bhedā<> pravāraṇāt karma /
Vin_4.14 / pravāraṇakaṃ saṃmanyeran* bhikṣuṃ /
Vin_4.15 / apāraṇe nekaṃ /
Vin_4.16 / nyāyam atrāṃśasaḥ paṃktau vyāpāraṇaṃ /
Vin_4.17 / darbhānasau cārayet* /
Vin_4.18 / pravāraṇaṃ pratyanyena saṃghasya jñapanam* /
Vin_4.19 / pratibhikṣvā pravāraṇāt puratas tiṣṭhet* /
Vin_4.20 / tasmai pravāraṇaṃ triḥ /
Vin_4.21 / dvis tāvatā glāna(na)klāntiśayanāsanasaṃbhedakālātikrānti[43b5]sambādhasnaṃpattisaṃbhāvane /
Vin_4.22 / tāvatāpi sakṛt* /
Vin_4.23 / tenāparasmai niṣṭhitāyāṃ paṃktau /
Vin_4.24 / abhāve nyasmai /
Vin_4.25 / sarvasaṃghena prativārite etat tvasya saṃghe nivedanam* /
/ sādhu pravāritaṃ suṣṭhu pravāritam iti /
Vin_4.26 / sarve samarthayeyuḥ /
Vin_4.27 / yena tenāsūceḥ /
/ svakyena vastunā vastapravāraṇam ārabheta vacanato gṛhītvā<>ḥ [43b6] saṃghena labhyaṃ bhadantā evaṃ rūpeṇāpi vastunā varṣoṣitam
bhikṣusaṃghaṃ pravārayitum iti /
Vin_4.28 / ataḥ śrāmaṇerān* pravārayet* /
Vin_4.29 / tato bhikṣuṇīḥ /
Vin_4.30 / pravāritatvam adhiṣṭhāya gatasyārvāktatpravāraṇāyāsahakṛtau /
Vin_4.31 / na striyāṃ parivṛtyāpi /
Vin_4.32 / aśakyatāyām avasthātuṃ bhāgaprāptaṃ bhikṣum avalokayet
gaṇapravāraṇena /
Vin_4.33 / [44a1] / /pravārayed antarvarṣa prakramiṣyan* karaṇīyena /
Vin_4.34 / sthāpayitvāpi vastupudgalam ubhayam vā /
Vin_4.35 / pratīccheyur eṇām /
Vin_4.36 / sthāpanena nantyatām upanīya /
/ na haiva vayam āyusmann ity arthaṃ sanniṣaṇṇāḥ sannipattitāḥ kaccid āyusman* vastu sthāpayen na putgalam ity api tu śīlaviśuddhyarthaṃ poṣadha ukto bhagavatā dharmathiśuddhyarthaṃ pravāraṇā saāced ākāṃ[44a2]kṣasi pravārayeti /
Vin_4.37 / putgagalaṃ sthāpayen na na vastv iti vastu sthāpayet* putgalañ ceti
abhaṅgaḥ pratīṣṭaiḥ vyapalāpe sthāpanasya pratīṣṭatāyā sthāpitasya vā /
Vin_4.38 / naivaṃvidhaṃ kiñcid astītivāde mṛṣātvam atra pūrvasyāsya vā /
Vin_4.39 / kalikṛtāñ cet bhikṣūṇām āganam upagatāḥ śṛṇuyuḥ dvitripoṣadhātikrāntiś cet pravārayeyuḥ /
Vin_4.40 / asaṃpattau yañca [44a3] pāṇimaṇḍakāni saṃmanyeran* /
Vin_4.41 / vākyasvalpakena pratyutgamya pātracīvarapratiśamanaṃ layanam ālaṃkakūṭāgāroddeśaḥ /
Vin_4.42 / snātrasnehalābhakaraṇaṃ /
Vin_4.43 / karaṇadharmaśravaṇadā(da)nam ity eṣāṃ pralobhanāni prayuñjīran* asaṃpattāv ātmībhāvasya poṣadhaṃ kurvīran* maṇḍalakeṣu /
Vin_4.44 / nanu yuṣmākam adya pravāraṇeti bruvāṇā[44a4]nām āgamayatāyuṣmantāgantukā yūyaṃ naivāsikā anenārtheneti prativadeyuḥ /
Vin_4.45 / prakrānteṣu pravāraṇām /
// pravāraṇāvastu // 1 //

**(Vin_4,2) kṣudrakādigatam /
Vin_4.46 / nākṛtakṣamaṇaḥ sāntarasya pravārayet* /
Vin_4.47 / daśārddhamāsena bhaviṣyattāyām asyās tatkālaḥ /
Vin_4.48 / saptāṣṭair ity aparaḥ /
Vin_4.49 / na sannipātaḥ /
Vin_4.50 / nāsāvakṣāntvānākṛtasaṃmodanasaṃni[44a5]hitānāṃ sarvas tadā /
Vin_4.51 / na ruṣitaṃ kṣamayet* /
Vin_4.52 / na bhikṣuṇī bhikṣuṃ bahirāvāsāt* /
Vin_4.53 / na pādayor nipatya /
Vin_4.54 / kṣānte niyatya gamanaṃ /
Vin_4.55 / naināṃ kṣamayan*tīmanādṛ(dṛ)tya bhikṣur gacchet* /
Vin_4.56 / na vilaṃghayet* /
Vin_4.57 / saṃjñapteḥ kṣamanīyasya purastād dāpanam abhijñāna /
Vin_4.58 / nāniṣṭāv upāyaparyeṣaṇaṃ nāpadyet* /
Vin_4.59 / na cīrayet* /
Vin_4.60 / na parya[44a6]vasthānāpagatin nodīkṣet* /
Vin_4.61 / na kṣamyamāṇo na kṣameta /
// kṣudrakādigataṃ // 2 //
// samāptañ ca pravāraṇavastu // 4 //

*Vin_5. kaṭhinavastu /
**(Vin_5,1) kṣudrakādigatam /
Vin_5.1 / āstrīṇvīran* kaṭhinam* /
Vin_5.2 / yathā trayam evam āstīrṇasya paraṃparabhojanam api nirdoṣaṃ gaṇabhojanaman āmantryagrāmapraveśaś cīvaravijñapanañ ca /
Vin_5.3 / sādhāraṇyam asya śiṣṭaiḥ lābhasya /
Vin_5.4 / anutthānam asyāvārṣi[44b1]kachinnavarṣapaścimavarṣasthānāntaroṣitavarṣeṣu bhūmyantarastheṣu ca /
Vin_5.5 / viṣṭhānam etat prāptau /
Vin_5.6 / bhāgino vyantyaśrāmaṇerabhūmyantarasthālābhe /
Vin_5.7 / notkṣiptaḥ /
Vin_5.8 / tattāprāptivad adharmapakṣeṣu yāto bhinneṣu /
Vin_5.9 / maulakālapravāraṇaparyantavarṣānimittakāstārakādinaparyantasambandhī cīvaralābhasaṃkhyaṃ ca tricīvaram /
Vin_5.10 / sāṃghikam amṛditam avi[44b2]likhitam apailotikam /
Vin_5.11 / na na varṇitakam* /
Vin_5.12 / aparibhuktaṃ /
Vin_5.13 / dṛḍham* /

Vin_5.16 / chinnasyūtam* /

Vin_5.18 / uttare vā /
Vin_5.19 / anāstīrṇapūrvañ ca /
Vin_5.20 / āstīrṇam* /
Vin_5.21 / anekam api /
Vin_5.22 / yāvat tadāstārakaḥ /
Vin_5.23 / cīvarāntarā[44b3]dhiṣṭhānam etat tasmād uddhṛtyādhiṣṭhitāni /
Vin_5.24 / rocayeran* sāmagryām* /

Vin_5.33 / nādyasya hānāv anutthānam* /

Vin_5.35 / sannipātagatānuṣṭhānam* /
Vin_5.36 / gandhapuṣpārcitaṃ surabhidhūpadhūpita cāṃgeripaṭalakastham ekaṃ trivānekam ādāya vṛddhā[44b5]nte vasthitenāstṛtes sampādanaṃ pratipadiḥ /
Vin_5.37 / kārtikasya /
Vin_5.38 / trir uktyā /
Vin_5.39 / āstṛṇomīti /
Vin_5.40 / pratibhikṣum agrataḥ sthitvā āstṛtamiti nivedanam /
Vin_5.41 / sādhv āstṛtaṃ suṣṭhv āstṛtaṃ yo tra lābhaś cānuśaṃsaś ca so 'smākamitītaraḥ /
Vin_5.42 / pratyanubhūtivad asyānumodanam* /

Vin_5.53 / udgatau niradhiṣṭhatre kartv antaḥsīmno 'raṇasya /

Vin_5.70 / āchitteḥ matve /
Vin_5.71 / nānuddhṛte sarveṣāṃ tātkālikaṃ lābhaṃ bhājayet* /

**(Vin_5,2) pṛcchāgatam /

Vin_5.83 / tad apacyutir uddhāraḥ /
Vin_5.84 / tasmād a[45a4]datvā cchandaṃ svapnasamāpatyoḥ saṃniṣaṇṇe syānutthānam āstārasyoddhṛteś ca prāk śruvaṇāt* /
Vin_5.85 / uṣitatvam ekasīmatāyāṃ tatrāvāsāntaroṣitānām āstāre /
Vin_5.86 / tatsthānatvam āstārakāle syām asya /
Vin_5.87 / yat tad āstṛtya pṛthak sīmakaraṇe cāsya sthānam* /

Vin_5.89 / pratipakṣaṃ bhinnatāyām* /

*Vin_6, cīvaravastu /
**(Vin_6,1) cīvaravastu /
Vin_6.1 / nāśastralūnaṃ vāsaḥ paribhuñjīta /
Vin_6.2 / chinnasyūtaṃ cīvaratvāyādhiṣṭhet /
Vin_6.3 / bhakticitratāśeṣa[45a6]samamadhyānyat tadgatapatramukhatvaparimaṇḍitatveḥ /
Vin_6.4 / antaravāsa uttaravāsaṃgaṃ saṃghāṭīñ ca /
Vin_6.5 / kūsulakasaṃghakṣike ca yat tadvidhe bhikṣuṇī /
Vin_6.6 / matasaṃbhave yācñāyāpi /
Vin_6.7 / naitad vihāsarutodgatim āgamayet /
Vin_6.8 / rohaty anyāsaṃpattāvaraktakasyādhiṣṭhānaṃ /
Vin_6.9 / achinnakasya ca /
Vin_6.10 / āsevakānām atra dānaṃ saṃbhavaś cet /
Vin_6.11 / [45b1] āgārikavidhasya ca /
Vin_6.12 / namatakocavaprāvārasthūlakambalapailātikam acchinnam āsaivakadānasūtam /
Vin_6.13 / tatkṣaṇād evāśucimrakṣaṇaṃ sampattau śayanāsanaṃ śocayeta /
Vin_6.14 / nainaṃ sāṃghikam akhaṭamaṃcapīṭhamapratyāstṛtamatenāniṣādāt saṃvaraṇaṃ vā dattāntarddhānam upabhuñjīta /
Vin_6.15 / sarvañ ca citram abhūyo vinaṣṭaṃ /
Vin_6.16 / na kalpabhūte[45b2]na malavavatā vā /
Vin_6.17 / dhāraṇaṃ pratyāstaraṇasya yena ekapuṭaṃ nyāyyam /
Vin_6.18 / dvipuṭaṃ pailotikam /
Vin_6.19 / akalpikaṃ citropacitraṃ /
Vin_6.20 / patramukham asya kurvīt* /
Vin_6.21 / adhas tṛtīyabhāgādau /
Vin_6.22 / naikakhaṇḍam adhitiṣṭhet /
Vin_6.23 / kaṇḍūpratichādanaṃ tadvān dhārayet /
Vin_6.24 / pañcayair enad davisaiḥ śocayet /
Vin_6.25 / kalpate kośeyamūrṇakaṃ śānakaṃ [45b3] kṣaumakañ ca /
Vin_6.26 / nātantotabhāṃgeyam /
Vin_6.27 / keśamayanāgnyaulūkapakṣikatvasamādānam /
Vin_6.28 / sthūlam atra /
Vin_6.29 / anyad etat bhajanam /
Vin_6.30 / keśaluñcanaparṇaśāṭyajinasāntarottarayāpanatiriṭāṅganāḍīsarvanīlapravāraṇadīrghadaśaphaṇadaśakaṃcukoṣṇīṣaśiroveṣṭanakutapoṣṭaka balatīrthikadhvajañ ca /
Vin_6.31 / pulāsapatrapūradīpavarti[45b4]kāmātratayāpi samatayai vibhajanam /
Vin_6.32 / vikrīyakocavatad vidhānām /
Vin_6.33 / na pāṭayitvā /
Vin_6.34 / pañcānāṃ labheḥ bhājane karaṇam adyalābho bhājayiṣyate tatra yuṣmābhiḥ sannipatitavyam ity ārocanaṃ saṃghe /
Vin_6.35 / gaṇḍyā koṭanam /
Vin_6.36 / śalākācāraṇam /
Vin_6.37 / gaṇanam /
Vin_6.38 / pratyaṃśapravāraṇaṃ /
Vin_6.39 / īśitvakriyamāṇatāyāmāntyādi[45b5]gatasya /
Vin_6.40 / nāvasitatve /
Vin_6.41 / kulābhake py etat /
Vin_6.42 / nānarhaḥ prakrāntāyāṃ tallābhakriyā praviṣṭeḥ /
Vin_6.43 / tasmān niyuñjīt* grahaṇe prakrāman /
Vin_6.44 / dasyutvam agrahaṇe pratijñātavataḥ /
Vin_6.45 / paṇapañcakāt prabhṛti kulābhake /
Vin_6.46 / nānukto gṛhṇīyāt /
Vin_6.47 / gṛhṇīyād ācāryopādhyāyo vā /
Vin_6.48 / viśrambhasthānārthañ ca /
Vin_6.49 / nāsvapakṣārthaṃ /
Vin_6.50 / [45b6] śayanāsane py etat /
Vin_6.51 / bhakte vā /
Vin_6.52 / parasparārthaṃ gṛhṇan vijñapayet /
Vin_6.53 / nānābhavan tam antarbhūyaḥ /
Vin_6.54 / naikatvam arddhasya suvarutā ca labdher anarhapraveśe kāraṇaṃ /
Vin_6.55 / anarhaḥ saṃghalābhasyādharmapakṣeṣu patito bhinneṣu /
Vin_6.56 / uṣitatvaṃ bahutaram uṣitasya tatkālake lābhe hānāyāsyāvṛttau mṛtyau ca /
Vin_6.57 / yathāviniyatilābhasya vyavasthā /
Vin_6.58 / [46a1] labdhṛbhiś ca /
Vin_6.59 / kṛtsnapratipādane pi /
Vin_6.60 / karmasīmnā saṃghasyāparicchede paricchedaḥ /
Vin_6.61 / tattvam atraikādeḥ /
Vin_6.62 / dharmalābhe tadbhāṇakānām īśitvam /
Vin_6.63 / ekārṣagāthādhāraṇaṃ tattve tra paryantaḥ /
Vin_6.64 / arhatvaṃ bhinnavyañjanasyetarasannidhau mṛtapariṣkāre /
Vin_6.65 / tathotkṣiptasya /
Vin_6.66 / asannidhau vā nivṛtte nimittāc cetasi /
Vin_6.67 / abhinnatvam asya tārādīyamaitadgrā[46a2]hyatāyāṃ /
Vin_6.68 / bhinnatvaṃ bhinnasya /
Vin_6.69 / nānyasya pravrajitāt sabrahmacāriṇas tadīśitvam /
Vin_6.70 / na jñaptyādhiṣṭhite prāptasya pūrvacarameṇa vā /
Vin_6.71 / kasyacit tataḥ saṃghavṛddhanavakayoḥ dānaṃ tad ākhyaṃ /
Vin_6.72 / yatrādhiṣṭheyasya gatatā tatsīmāntargatānām adhiṣṭhatṛtvam /
Vin_6.73 / akaraṇam atra maraṇasthānatā /
Vin_6.74 / sīmāntarikāt sthalagne kāye nyatra vā yātāmā[46a3]krāntis tāvad gatānāṃ /
Vin_6.75 / saprativastukatve yatrāsau tadgatatvaṃ pariskārasya /
Vin_6.76 / prativastukenānyastham adhitiṣṭheyuḥ /
Vin_6.77 / preṣitasyāpratikṣiptasya saṃpradānena tadīyatvam /
Vin_6.78 / pratikṣiptasya preṣayitṛtvam /
Vin_6.79 / pratikṣiptasyāpi tena /
Vin_6.80 / bahir asya rūḍhiḥ /
Vin_6.81 / sīmno ntaḥ saṃjñinā kevalādhiṣṭhānam /
Vin_6.82 / nākṛte nirhārasatkaraṇadharmaśravaṇadakṣi[46a4]ṇādeśane dhitiṣṭhiteyuḥ /
Vin_6.83 / antargṛhasthatve pātracīvarasya yasmai gṛhapatinā dānaṃ tasyaiśitvam /
Vin_6.84 / arhaś cet /
Vin_6.85 / vihīnaś ca tena /
Vin_6.86 / adāne yācitavataḥ /
Vin_6.87 / krame prathamam /
Vin_6.88 / asattve nuddeśatvāt pṛṣṭau gatavataḥ /
Vin_6.89 / tadvat krame /
Vin_6.90 / enikodbhūto taddeyaparimāṇasya tadgāmitvaṃ mṛtapariskārasya /
Vin_6.91 / vibhaktasyāpi /

Vin_8.205 / na rājyam upārdham vāsya pratīccheta /

Vin_8.349 / tatkālārtham aparopasthāpanam /

Vin_8.351 / caturṇām api [53b3] śleṣmakaṭakasthāpanam /

Vin_8.383 / karaṇaṃ chīdrapīṭhasya codanāroge /
Vin_8.384 / saṃvartanena bālasya /
Vin_8.385 / asaṃpattau chedanam* /
Vin_8.386 / sāmantake duḥkhanaṃ cet pātravaibhaṅgukānāṃ dānam* /
Vin_8.387 / rakṣyo bhūmināśas tasmād aṣkaryakarasya /
Vin_8.388 / [53b6] nānyuccā sādhu /
Vin_8.389 / kālena kālam adurgandhatāyai śocanam* /
Vin_8.390 / śoṣaṇaṃ mrakṣaṇañ ca kaṭukatailena /
Vin_8.391 / tatkālārtham aparārjanam* /
Vin_8.392 / asaṃpattau patalikādhāratvenopayogaḥ /
Vin_8.393 / kṛtvoccāraṃ tatkaraṇaśuddhet* /
Vin_8.394 / na tīkṣṇena tṛṇakurvakena vā /
Vin_8.395 / natukapattalikapatravaibhaṅgukaloṣṭhakāṣṭhānām atra sādhutvam /
Vin_8.396 / dvābhyāṃ ca mṛdbhyāṃ śocayet /
Vin_8.397 / prāk sthāpitābhiḥ [54a1] / /pravibhāgena mṛdbhir uttaraḥ śocaḥ /
Vin_8.398 / sanair mandamandamanāśayatāviskambhinācamanikāpādukām /
Vin_8.399 / saptabhir vāmasya /
Vin_8.400 / saptabhir ubhayoḥ vāhviḥ śocanam* /
Vin_8.401 / punaḥ hastayor mṛdā /
Vin_8.402 / aparāyā[ḥ] kuṇḍikāyāḥ pādaprakṣālanam(a) /
Vin_8.403 / nirdoṣaṃ śūte kukṣeḥ prāgantāt poccanamātraṃ kṛtvāsanaṃ nāto nyaḥ /
Vin_8.404 / saty udake nāvānte niṣīdet* /

*Vin_9, karmavastu /
**(Vin_9,1) karmavastu /
Vin_9.1 / vidhyutkrame karmaṇo rūḍhiḥ /
Vin_9.2 / nāśrāpyaśruto /
Vin_9.3 / nārūḍhi kuryāt* /
Vin_9.4 / jñaptivācanāprātimokṣoddeśapravāraṇās tat /
Vin_9.5 / nādharmeṇa kuryuḥ /
Vin_9.6 / na vyagrāḥ /
Vin_9.7 / na gaṇasya /
Vin_9.8 / nāsaṃghabhūtāḥ /
Vin_9.9 / viṃ*śatiprabhṛtīnām āvartaṇe saṃghatvaṃ /
Vin_9.10 / upasaṃpadi daśaprabhṛtīnāṃ /
Vin_9.11 / vinayadharapañcamādīnāṃ pratyanteṣv asaṃpattau /
Vin_9.12 / śiṣṭe catuḥ[54a3]prabhṛtīnām* hiruktvaṃ bhikṣuṇīnāṃ /
Vin_9.13 / karmaṇi pravāraṇaṃ bhikṣusaṃghe pi /
Vin_9.14 / poṣadhasaṃpannasāmagryāṇāṃ tena /
Vin_9.15 / chandapoṣadhaharaṇena tatsaṃpādanam* /
Vin_9.16 / dvayor atra vyāpṛtiḥ /
Vin_9.17 / pratibalatvam anayoḥ /
Vin_9.18 / abhāva ekasyāgrahītubhikṣusaṃghena niyogo bhikṣoḥ /
Vin_9.19 / dvārakoṣṭhake tenāvasthānam* /

Vin_9.21 / tenāsyetat /
Vin_9.22 / na palāyanama /
Vin_9.23 [54a4] ajñāto nāma gotrapraśnaḥ /
Vin_9.24 / mānāsyavartaṇaṃ dvayos sāme tayoḥ /
Vin_9.25 / upasaṃpādanañ ca /
Vin_9.26 / dvādaśavargo trāsāṃ /
Vin_9.27 / sapūrvasaṃvṛtidvayaparṣadanalaparṣadupasthānasaṃvṛtidāne 'ntaḥ saṃghasya /

Vin_9.30 / nāsanniṣādasthasya pūrakatvam* /
Vin_9.31 / na yasya kriyateḥ [54a5] tasmād asatvaṃ pūrakatvasya chandapariśuddhir vidheḥ /
Vin_9.32 / arhat*tvam anayoḥ /
Vin_9.33 / asammatiprakārakatvena /
Vin_9.34 / nānupasaṃpatkadhvastānantaryakṛtpāpadṛṣṭibhūmyentarasthanānāsaṃvāsikānām* /
Vin_9.35 / saskhalitasya ca /
Vin_9.36 / saṃvarakaraṇīyenāpi /
Vin_9.37 / bhavaty adhiṣṭhānena śuddhatvam* /
Vin_9.38 / na śakyatāyām* /
Vin_9.39 / śakyatvaṃ tadātane śuddhaprāyaścittikapratideśanīyaduḥkṛtapratikaraṇasya pratigra[54a6]hītṛsadbhāve deśanāmātrakatvāt* /
Vin_9.40 / yathā saṃgham āpanne pratipadyet /
Vin_9.41 / nyāyyam evaṃ nāśanaṃ caikasya /
Vin_9.42 / pratikaraṇañ cānekadhā /
Vin_9.43 / naiṣāṃ kartṛtvaṃ /
Vin_9.44 / uddeṣṭṭatvaṃ sāvaśeṣaṃ pratikriyāyāṃ /

Vin_9.46 / utsṛjya varjitam anāvṛttaṃ /
Vin_9.47 / utkṣiptañ ca svakarmaṇi /
Vin_9.48 / annaḥ pṛcchārthaṃ jñaptiprabhṛtau copadyamānaṃ /

Vin_9.52 / nājñapite tadarthaṃ vācanā /
Vin_9.53 / tatsīmāntargatasyārhasya pūraṇe kāyataḥ chandato vā saṃniṣāde nanupraviṣṭatvaṃ pratikroṣantā ca yasya tatkarma tato nyasya pratikūlaṃ cet dharmaṃ vācyutasyeryāpathāt* pra[54b2]kṛtisthasya saṃyatasya vā cotsṛjyānabhijñasāntarāt* vyagratvaṃ /
Vin_9.54 / mṛṣāvādaprahvatvam asaṃyatir vācā /

Vin_9.59 / nānyatra /

Vin_9.64 / na niyamya kālaṃ paunaḥpunye nyatra vā /
Vin_9.65 / dadhyur anyatra yāvad arthaṃ parihāraṃ /
Vin_9.66 / śalākagrahaṇenābhāve saṃmatasya bhājanam /

*Vin_10, pratikriyāvastu /
**(Vin_10,1) pratikriyāvastu /
Vin_10.1 / nāpratikṛtājñapanajaṣkarma pratyanubhavet /
Vin_10.2 / utsṛjya poṣadhaṃ pravāraṇāñ ca /
Vin_10.3 / na sīmāntarasthasya kasmiṃś cid aṅgatvam /
Vin_10.4 / dhvaṃsas tadgatau sāhya gatasya /
Vin_10.5 / ubhayasthatvam ekasminn e[55a4]katra pāde parasmin paratra /
Vin_10.6 / sarvasminn avaṣṭambhini sthitasyāvaṣṭabdhe /
Vin_10.7 / rūḍhir evam anekatropagateḥ /
Vin_10.8 / arhatvam anekaśayanāsanagrāhe /
Vin_10.9 / yatheṣṭam asya vastavyatā /
Vin_10.10 / na vyagrakāritvaṃ jinasya /
Vin_10.11 / na pūrakatvam /
Vin_10.12 / nākarmaṇā tatkaraṇīyasyotthānam /
Vin_10.13 / kṛtatvaṃ yadbhūyas kṛtatve vākyasyānuttarasya /
Vin_10.14 / nākīrttitve nimittānāṃ bandhe /
Vin_10.15 / pārivāsike [55a5] nāntasyopasthānasaṃvṛteḥ /
Vin_10.16 / unmattakena coddeśasya /
Vin_10.17 / jñaptivad bhedānuṣṭhānam /
Vin_10.18 / anaṅgam atra bhinnavyaṃjanatvam /
Vin_10.19 / na hāsyabhāvena kasyacit sthūlam arūḍhibuddhyā bhedotkṣepayoḥ /
Vin_10.20 / duṣkṛtam asaṃghabhūtatve /
Vin_10.21 / nānyeṣāṃ nānāsaṃvāsikebhyo barhāṇāṃ pūraṇe gaṇena jñaptivācanayoḥ /
Vin_10.22 / nāsaṃpannatve 'rha[ḥ] svasaṃghena pratyanubhavasya /
Vin_10.23 / saṃpannatvaṃ [55a6] jñaptiśrutāv asya nāvidhir bhavyarūpe pratinidhinā dūtena pravrājanam /
Vin_10.24 / uttarañ copasaṃpādanāt /

Vin_10.26 / dhvaṃso 'tra yācanasya /
Vin_10.27 / vidhitvaṃ mevakajñapanapūrvakatve 'sya /
Vin_10.28 / utkṣepe 'py etat /
Vin_10.29 / avadhānaṃ pareṇāsamanvāhārād yukto tantraḥ /
Vin_10.30 / nārthacchedānā, kramavyatyād arūḍhiḥ /
Vin_10.31 / akaraṇīyatvaṃ bhreṣasya /
Vin_10.32 / na vyañjanāntara[55b1]saṃśrayāt /
Vin_10.33 / na bhikṣubhikṣuṇītvayor anyakarmavastupratijñapite codakena kalpayati sāṃmukhyaṃ praṇidhikaraṇam /
Vin_10.34 / pratītimātreṇa sannipātādāne /
Vin_10.35 / anaṅgam adarśane vyāghātitvāt sattvasya pratijñānam /
Vin_10.36 / avakāśāṃ karaṇe cāyogāt /
Vin_10.37 / saṃpatyāsvayam anutthāne codakasyotthāpanam /
Vin_10.38 / [ā]kroṣaroṣakaparibhāṣakatāmalābhāvā[55b2]sābhyāṃ saṃghasya cetakatvam /
Vin_10.39 / rājakulayuktakulajñātipudgalapratisaraṇatām apratisartṛtāṃ saṃghasyābibhrataḥ /
Vin_10.40 / akurvāṇasyāsyāgārikatīrthikadhvajadhāraṇatīrthyasevānācāracaraṇānyaśikṣaṇañ ca bhikṣuśikṣāyām utkacaprakacasya saṃghe roma pātayato niḥsaraṇaṃ pravarttayataḥ samīcīm upadarśayato viramato nimittād avasāraṇaṃ yācite /
Vin_10.41 / [55b3] karmadānabarhaṇopasaṃpādanapratiprasrambhannonmajjanañ ca /
Vin_10.42 / kalahakārakatam jayeyuḥ karmaṇā /
Vin_10.43 / nigarhaṇam abhīkṣṇasaṃghāvaśeṣāpattikasyāpratikṛtya /
Vin_10.44 / kuladūṣakasya pravāsanam /
Vin_10.45 / adānākaraṇayoś ca tadarthaṃ saṃnipātāvakāśayoḥ /
Vin_10.46 / udbhāvane ca tadadṛṣṭeḥ /
Vin_10.47 / pratisaṃharaṇamavam paṇḍitāgārikasya /
Vin_10.48 / tatkṣama[55b4]ṇakam atra karmaṇaḥ sthāne 'vasāraṇaṃ prati pratītāyām[ā]pattāvapratikṛtāyām apratikāryāyāṃ saṃvareṇādṛṣṭim udbhāvayantam anicchantaṃ pratikṛtim anuṣṭhātum anutsṛjantaṃ ca pāpikāṃ dṛṣṭim utkṣipeyuḥ /
Vin_10.49 / ihaivainām āpattiṃ pratikurvīthā ayam eva tv āsaṃghaḥ prasrambhayiṣyati ity evaṃ brūyyuḥ /
Vin_10.50 / nāpattiṃ praticchādayet /
Vin_10.51 / nāmnā 'ntataḥ [55b5] pravedyatvam /
Vin_10.52 / yathākathaṃcit duṣkṛtasya /
Vin_10.53 / prakṛtisthe /
Vin_10.54 / ananyadṛṣṭau sopasaṃpadi /
Vin_10.55 / tulyavyaṃjane /
Vin_10.56 / ataivaitat sottaram /
Vin_10.57 / kṛtatvam asyaidaṃdharmake /
Vin_10.58 / sīmāntarasthe ca /
Vin_10.59 / saṃghe sarvatrājñāpanajānām /
Vin_10.60 / sannihite tatrāsrame pratideśanīyasya garhyam āyuṣmantaḥ sthānam āpanno sātmyaṃ pratideśanīyanta dharmaṃ pratide[śa]yāmi iti /
Vin_10.61 / naitan mantravat /
Vin_10.62 / [55b6] saṃvarakṛter ato vyutthānaṃ mānasītaḥ /
Vin_10.63 / anya tasmai tado deśanāt /
Vin_10.64 / ekatra /
Vin_10.65 / ananyadṛṣṭo tatra /
Vin_10.66 / asamāvanye nikāyataḥ /
Vin_10.67 / abhāve āpattitaḥ /
Vin_10.68 / niḥsargavīcanapūrvakānaiḥkātaḥ /
Vin_10.69 / saṃghe sthūlāt sarvatra /
Vin_10.70 / paṃcakādau saśeṣāgatād guruṇaḥ /
Vin_10.71 / aśeṣāgatād anavacchinne bhūyasi /
Vin_10.72 / liṅghorasmāc catuṣkādau /
Vin_10.73 / kṛta[56a1] / /vadante 'trodyuktasyāsaṃpannaprayatve karma /
Vin_10.74 / duṣkāravattvamūḍhakṛtasya pratyāpattau saṃjñāyamānasya tena /
Vin_10.75 / nāmagotropasaṃhitam āpattitvāt kīrttanam /
Vin_10.76 / iyatkālapraticchannatayā vā saṃghāvaśeṣāyām /
Vin_10.77 / āvarhaṇam ato vyutthānakṛta /
Vin_10.78 / caritamānāsyasya /
Vin_10.79 / ṣaḍ aham ādāya saṃghāt /
Vin_10.80 / arddhamāsaṃ bhikṣuṇyāḥ /
Vin_10.81 / gurudharmā[56a2]tikrame 'py asya caritatvam /
Vin_10.82 / asati praticchādadoṣe tad rūḍhiḥ /
Vin_10.83 / parivāena tadapahatiḥ /
Vin_10.84 / tāvantaṃ kālam ād[ā]ya saṃghāt /
Vin_10.85 / kriyamāntāyām anayos tatsaṃghāvaśeṣāpadane dhvaṃsaḥ kṛtādānayoḥ /
Vin_10.86 / tasmān mūlopakramatvaṃ dānam /
Vin_10.87 / nirvāhya tatprastutam /
Vin_10.88 / tasmād arūḍhasyāsya pṛthak tadānīm utthāpyatā prathamaṃ ca /
Vin_10.89 / pratikāryaṃ tadāntaram /
Vin_10.90 / tasmāt tādarthasyā[56a3]pi saṃśrayatvam /
Vin_10.91 / avarodhyatā cātiriktasya tatpraticchādakālasya /
Vin_10.92 / karmaṇā nyoddānam /
Vin_10.93 / āvarhaṇāñ ca /
Vin_10.94 / tarjanaṃ cātra jñaptiprathamavācanāntarāle /
Vin_10.95 / nipatitasya tṛṇaprastārakeṇa /
Vin_10.96 / samudrejanañ ca /
Vin_10.97 / kṛtatotkīrttanāntaram /
// [iti] pratikriyāvastu // 1 //

**(Vin_10,2) kṣudrādigatam /
Vin_10.98 / niṣkāśanaṃ duḥśīlasya /
Vin_10.99 / saṃghasyātra pragamaḥ /
Vin_10.100 / nāsāvenadavyupekṣeta /
Vin_10.101 / [56a4] avasāryatvaṃ nāśitasya /
Vin_10.102 / nāsāṃ manye praṇidhātṝṇām avasāraṇasya praṇihitau rūḍhiḥ /
Vin_10.103 / avastavyatā dūṣitasthāne pravāsitasya /
Vin_10.104 / sarvatrotkṣiptake saṃbāsyatvāsaṃbhogyatve /
Vin_10.105 / saṃjñayātra vyavasthānam /
Vin_10.106 / adharmapakṣasyaitibhinnatāyām itareṇa /
Vin_10.107 / nānyasya /
Vin_10.108 / nānyatraita praṇihite /
Vin_10.109 / apāśrayeṇāsya vastavyatā sapremakasya /
Vin_10.110 / vikṛteḥ kriyamāṇapraṇidhinā dhvaste[56a5]na ca niṣkāsya mānena bhajane bhāṇḍasya choraṇam /
Vin_10.111 / valāniṣkāśaḥ /
Vin_10.112 / avalambanasya chodanam /
Vin_10.113 / apatanadharmaṇā tatrotpāṭanam /
Vin_10.114 / saṃghena tasya pratisaṃskaraṇam /
Vin_10.115 / saṃpradāsya /
Vin_10.116 / asaṃpattau vaihārāt /
Vin_10.117 / na kalahakārakaṃ niṣkāsyamānan vārayet /
Vin_10.118 / anivṛttau kaler upaśāntyai prayatnād utkṣepaḥ /
Vin_10.119 / viniścayagate vyupaśamanena /
Vin_10.120 / niḥśrite niḥśrayaḥ praya[56a6]tet /
Vin_10.121 / nimittasyāpi kalerupasaṃhāriṇotkṣepyatā /
Vin_10.122 / saṃsṛṣṭavihāriṇam api bhikṣuṇībhir utkṣipeyuḥ /
Vin_10.123 / avandanārhasaṃvṛtim atrotkṣiptasya bhikṣuṇyāṣ kuryuḥ /
Vin_10.124 / udbhavo 'nyasya praṇidhiḥ nimitte tadarthābhisandhināny aprakṛtau /
Vin_10.125 / arūḍhir anyathātvaṃ paratra /
Vin_10.126 / anutthānam utkṣepe /
Vin_10.127 / sthūlaṃ jñātamahāpuṇyasūtravinayamātṛkādharabahuśrutapakṣam anivārāṇāṃ [56b1] nirdoṣanāgārikabhikṣvādipañcakāvaspaṇḍane 'pi pratisaṃharaṇam /
Vin_10.128 / nākrośyenāvaspaṇḍanam /
Vin_10.129 / anāśaṃkyaṃ svasādhāraṇyam /
Vin_10.130 / anupasaṃpatkasyaiṣāṃ pravrajite kartavyatā /
Vin_10.131 / na gṛhiṇi /
Vin_10.132 / pātrasasvākhyātāraṃ prati bhikṣor abhūtena pārājaikena /
Vin_10.133 / krośakaṃ paribhāṣakaṃ ca nikubjayeran /
Vin_10.134 / vyavasthākaraṇataḥ /
Vin_10.135 / prajñaptyā /
Vin_10.136 / na nikubjitayā tasya [56b2] gṛhān gacchet /
Vin_10.137 / nāsanaṃ paribhuñjīta /
Vin_10.138 / na prajñaptān deyadharmaṃ /
Vin_10.139 / na piṇḍapātaṃ pratigṛhṇītāt /
Vin_10.140 / na dharmaṃ deśayet /
Vin_10.141 / yat karma karaṇaṃ tadgatānāṃ nikubjitatvam /
Vin_10.142 / anuttānam asyāsvapakṣakulaṃ pratyotkṣiptakāt /
Vin_10.143 / tetanamasya kenacit /
Vin_10.144 / kṣamitataty unmajjanaṃ jñapanena /
Vin_10.145 / bhavaty utthānam anutpannapraticchādacittasyāntimātaḥ /
Vin_10.146 / śikṣācaraṇena /
Vin_10.147 / [56b3] tallabhāyāḥ saṃghataḥ /
Vin_10.148 / karmaṇā dānam /
Vin_10.149 / yāvaj jīva[m] /
Vin_10.150 / śuddhir ekasya purato deśanena saṃghāvaśeṣato hrīmataḥ /
Vin_10.151 / sūtradharasya vinayasya mātṛkāyāḥ /
Vin_10.152 / jñātasya ca /
Vin_10.153 / aśayatāpattivyutthānena daṇḍakarmataḥ /
Vin_10.154 / nikāyato nāmātrāpatter nāma /
Vin_10.155 / samutthānaṃ gotram /
// samāptaṃ pratikriyāvastu // 10 //

*Vin_11, kālākālasampātavastu /
**(Vin_11,1) kālākālasampātavstu /
Vin_11.1 / apratītatve saṃghāvaśeṣāntardhāne [56b4] ntāsthitapratichādacittasyāśaktavattāyāṃ kṛtaṃ ne vā kiṃ* vā kīdṛśyaṃ ceti smartum anupasaṃpa katotkṣiptayoś cānutthānaṃ pratichādasya /
Vin_11.2 / bhraṣṭasyāvahārikasaṃjñatāyām āpatter asyāparājayāt* /
Vin_11.3 / aprajñaptatāyāṃ ca /
Vin_11.4 / nājñātatvena sraddhitatve vā /
Vin_11.5 / anabhijñatāsaṃjñino pi /
Vin_11.6 / bhūmyantarasthitāyāṃ prāco pi /
Vin_11.7 / jñānavat pratichāde vimatiḥ saṃghā[56b5]vaśeṣatvaṃ /
Vin_11.8 / āvaraṇasyāpi sābhūti yā pratichādānutthānasya /
Vin_11.9 / duṣkṛtam anādṛtyaiḥ caraṇotsarge /
Vin_11.10 / tanaikāyikādhyācāre cātra /
Vin_11.11 / saṃbhave cāpratikṛtau /
Vin_11.12 / tadavasthatvaṃ pratyāgatāvacaraṇabhūmeḥ /
Vin_11.13 / śodhite vastuni sāṣānuṣṭhānam anirjñāne pratichādakālasyāsaṃvya ānany ūnatvasya saṃśrayaṇaṃ /
Vin_11.14 / caritavyatāyāṃ śuddhāntikatvottarasya /
Vin_11.15 / catu[56b6]ro māsāṃ śuddhāntikam iti /
Vin_11.16 / aparimātvasyāpratichāde /
Vin_11.17 / saṃcintya śukre visṛṣṭa-samutthāma-parimāṇām iti /
Vin_11.18 / yāvatīṣv abhiprāyas tāvat kīmitvam atrātrānuṣṭhiteḥ /
Vin_11.19 / aparimāna ity anirjñāne sya saṃśrayasaṃbahulāḥ parimānavatya iti prābhūtye /
Vin_11.20 / atiriktena kālānāṃ /
Vin_11.21 / prabhṛtimatvena nāmnāṃ /
Vin_11.22 / gurutvatīvrāśayakṛtatvā[57a1] //bhyām āditvena /
Vin_11.23 / carato paraprāksampannapraticikīrṣotpattau pṛ[tha]g* dānam ekaṃ caraṇaṃ /
Vin_11.24 / nāsya pratichannatāyāṃ mānāsye saṃbhavaḥ /
// [iti] kālākālasaṃpātavastu // 1 //

**(Vin_11,2) pṛcchāgatam /
Vin_11.25 / nānantye nse horātrasya pratichādotthānam* /
Vin_11.26 / nābhāve ṅgasyodbhāvanāyātmacittānā[ṃ] pratichādaḥ /
Vin_11.27 / abhāvamamatyapakrāntivaśasya /
Vin_11.28 / tadarthavaśatayāpi kṛtau /
Vin_11.29 / vinārthe[57a2]na duṣkṛtam /
Vin_11.30 / prātkānhyāt /
Vin_11.31 / anutsṛṣṭatvaṃ pratichādacittasya tatcittatānadorṣamāpatteḥ parājitasyāprakṛtau /
// kālākālasaṃpātavastu pṛcchā // 11 //

*Vin_12, bhūmyantarasthacaraṇavastu /
**(Vin_12,1) bhūmyantarasthacaraṇavastu /
Vin_12.1 / pārivāsikamānāsyacāribhyām abhivādanavandana-pratyutthānāṃjalisāmīcīkarmaṇāṃ prakṛtisthād bhikṣor asvīkaraṇaṃ /
Vin_12.2 / yasyābhyāmakaraṇam itarair api tatra tadgatasya /
Vin_12.3 / yad aparihāṇikāto nyathānena sārddham acaṃkra[57a3]maṇam /
Vin_12.4 / nīcatarāsanakatvād aniṣādaḥ /
Vin_12.5 / paścācchramaṇātmakatātaṣkulānupasaṃkramaṇaṃ /
Vin_12.6 / akalpanamekachadane śayyāyāḥ /
Vin_12.7 / pravrājanopasaṃpādananiḥśrayadānaśramaṇoddeśopasthāpanānām akaraṇaṃ /
Vin_12.8 / prajñaptivācanayoś cāpratīṣṭaḥ /
Vin_12.9 / karmakārakabhikṣuṇyavavādakasaṃghavaiśvāsikasammateḥ /
Vin_12.10 / avyāparaṇa prāksammatenāpi /
Vin_12.11 / anavava[57a4]danañ ca bhikṣuṇīnām* /
Vin_12.12 / anuddeśaḥ poṣadhe prātimokṣasya saty anyatroddeṣṭari /
Vin_12.13 / acodanaṃ vipattyā bhikṣoḥ /
Vin_12.14 / anapasāritasya saṃghāt* /
Vin_12.15 / akaraṇaṃ savacanīyatāsakīlatvayoḥ /
Vin_12.16 / asthāpanam avavādapoṣadhapravāraṇājñaptivācanānāṃ /
Vin_12.17 / asaṃprayogo nena /
Vin_12.18 / varjanaṃ kṛtadaṇḍanimittasya /
Vin_12.19 / anyasya cāparādhasya /
Vin_12.20 / nāparādhyatā sabrahmacāriṣu /
Vin_12.21 / [57a5] vratasya niḥsāraḥ pravartito bhavatīti manasikaraṇaṃ /
Vin_12.22 / kālyam utthāya dvāramokṣo dīpasthālakoddharaṇavihārasekasaṃmārgasukumārigomayakārṣyānupradānāni /
Vin_12.23 / dhāvanaṃ prasrāvoccārakuṭyāḥ /
Vin_12.24 / poccana-mṛtakālānurūpapānīyopasthāpanam* /
Vin_12.25 / praṇāḍikāmukhānāṃ dhāvanam* /
Vin_12.26 / āsanaṃ prajñapanam* /
Vin_12.27 / kālaṃ jñātvā dhūpatatkaṭacchukayor upasthapanama /
Vin_12.28 / [57a6] pratibalatā vecchāsturguṇāsaṃkīrtaṇaṃ /
Vin_12.29 / na ced bhāṣaṇakādhyeṣaṇaṃ /
Vin_12.30 / upanvāhṛte gaṇḍīdānam* /
Vin_12.31 / dharmaś ced bhikṣūṇāṃ vījanam* /
Vin_12.32 / antyatvam asya sarvopasaṃpannānām /
Vin_12.33 / kṛte bhaktakṛtye śayanāsanasya channe gopanam* /
Vin_12.34 / pātrādhiṣṭhānachoraṇaṃ* /
Vin_12.35 / kālaṃ jñātvā stūpānāṃ saṃmārjanam* /
Vin_12.36 / sukumārigomayakārṣyanupradānaṃ /
Vin_12.37 / sāmagrīvelāyāṃ pra[57b1]jñapanādyāguṇagatāt* /
Vin_12.38 / pratibalatā ced divasārocanam* /
Vin_12.39 / na ced anyasya bhikṣor adhyeṣaṇaṃ /
Vin_12.40 / pādaśocanaṃ bhikṣūṇāṃ caikālikaṃ kālānurūpeṇāmbunā /
Vin_12.41 / mrakṣaṇañ cānicchāyāṃ snehopasaṃhāraḥ /
Vin_12.42 / vihāre 'sya pratyante rhatvaṃ /
Vin_12.43 / arhatvaṃ sarvatra lābhe /
Vin_12.44 / pratijāgriyāt kuśalapakṣe /
Vin_12.45 / tadvad atra tatprabhāvaiṣīyaśikṣādattakau /
[R om.] / naivoddeśaḥ /
/ avasāraṇena /
/ pūrvasya pra[57b2]kṛtigateḥ /
/ arhatvenottarasya /
/ prāg* dvāramokṣyād vihārādau ca paryuṣitavac caritapattau /
/ tathātaritapattau /
/ tathātarjitanigarhitaprathāsitapratisaṃkṛtotkṣiptāḥ /
/ naivoddeśaḥ /
/ varjanam evotkṣiptasyetaraiḥ /
/ anartatvañ ca tadātvanimittalābhe /
/ bhinnavat* /
/ tadvadbhinneṣv adharmapakṣyaḥ /
/ arūḍair aprakṛtistheṣu paripāsamānāpy aśikṣācaraṇānāṃ / [end of R om.]
Vin_12.46 / asaṃghe ca /
Vin_12.47 / [57b3] paricchinneṣu ca tadāśramapadopagebhyaḥ /
Vin_12.48 / na bahutāṃ pariharet* /
Vin_12.49 / sa sthaviraprātimokṣatāyai prayateta /
Vin_12.50 / na yatryānye triḥprabhṛtayaḥ sarvathā tadākhyacaraṇās tatra taccaret* /
Vin_12.51 / nānyatra prathamāvaraṇeṇānudgamayenāṃ /
Vin_12.52 / varttsyat vṛttam ārocayetāṃ /
Vin_12.53 / saṃnipāte saṃghasya /
Vin_12.54 / pratyahaṃ na cec ciraṃ caritavyatvaṃ /
Vin_12.55 / atra tricaturaiḥ /
Vin_12.56 / naivānenārthenāvaspaṇḍayet* /
Vin_12.57 / [57b4] kalahakārakāgamanañ ca śrutvā bhayañ cedataḥ pratini[ḥ]sṛjetāṃ saṃghasannidhau pudgale vā /
Vin_12.58 / apagatau bhīter ādānaṃ tatraivaṃ /
/ bhūmyantarasthacaraṇavastu // 1 //

**(Vin_12,2) pṛcchāgatam /
Vin_12.59 / chedas tadahorātrasya prakṛtisthena sārdham ekachadane parivāsikamānāsyacāriṇoḥ śayyāyāṃ bahi[ḥ]sīmni ca /
Vin_12.60 / anārocane ca /
Vin_12.61 / nāsannidhau tatsīmni śrāvyāṇām asyotthānaṃ nirdoṣaṃ tadaharā[57b5]gatau sīmāntare gamanam* /
Vin_12.62 / na parivāsikena sārdham ekachadane pārivāsikaḥ śayīt* /
Vin_12.63 / na tīrthyupanivāsasthasya tena sārdham atra doṣaḥ //
// bhūmyantarasthacaraṇavastupṛcchā // 12

*Vin_13. parikarmavastu
Vin_13.1 // nāprāsiddhikasya mūlatvaṃ /
Vin_13.2 / arūḍhir avasitapravāraṇoktau pravāraṇāsthāpanasya /
Vin_13.3 / tathā glānakartṛkatāyāṃ /
Vin_13.4 / dūtenāpi /
Vin_13.5 / glānagatāyāñ ca /
Vin_13.6 / [57b6] naitat pratīccheyuḥ /
Vin_13.7 / āgamaya tvam āyuṣmaṃ glānas tvam aprayojyama ity āyusmaṃ bhūteti glāno sāv ananuyojyā iti prativadeyuḥ /
Vin_13.8 / anavagatasvarūpatāyāṃ kṛtasya kartur vā codanasya /
Vin_13.9 / śiṣṭe pi nākāle pravarteta /
Vin_13.10 / nānupasthāsya smṛtisaṃprajanye /
Vin_13.11 / nānekānte /
Vin_13.12 / nākāritāvakāśe /
Vin_13.13 / tatvaṃ pravāraṇasya /
Vin_13.14 / asmṛtau smāraṇaṃ [58a1] /
Vin_13.15 // akaraṇebhyaḥ vacanīyatām asya kuryāt* /
Vin_13.16 / savacanīyaṃ tv āyuṣman karomi na tvaṃ yo smādāvāsādanavalokya prakramitavyam asti me āyuṣmati praṇihitaṃ vacanāyeti /
Vin_13.17 / āgacchaty eva damanāthamana codyatāṃ /
Vin_13.18 / ālapanāder asy anuvinivartanam* /
Vin_13.19 / tathāpi poṣadhasthāpanaṃ /
Vin_13.20 / tato pi pravāraṇāyāḥ /
Vin_13.21 / karaṇam asyatra sthāpakaiḥ sthāpitasya tena [58a2] sārdham upasāraṇaṃ /
Vin_13.22 / kṛtatve vakāśasyāmṛdutvaṃ cet sakīlakaraṇaṃ /
Vin_13.23 / vakṣyāmy atrāmutra vā vase mutra vā vāstuni yatra ceṣṭam ity āropya cāmattiṃ* darśayitvāparādham utsṛjanena /
Vin_13.24 / śīladṛṣṭyā cārājīva vipatyā sarvasyāsya codanādeḥ kriyāyāṃ ruḍhiḥ samūlakaṃ /
Vin_13.25 / na durdūlena kuryāt* /
Vin_13.26 / akaraṇam atra vastunaḥ satyatvaṃ /
Vin_13.27 / kriyānimittānāṃ parasaṃlāpa[58a3]sya sānuśrāvaṇasyeti trividhaṃ śrutaṃ /
Vin_13.28 / amūlatvam asraddhitasya /
Vin_13.29 / kāmo nekatve jñātuś codanādau /
Vin_13.30 / nāpravāraṇe tatsthāvanam* /
Vin_13.31 / nāpoṣadhe tasya na kṛtau kṛtatve vā strītve sthāpakasyai[ka]tarasya puṃstve sthāpitatvaṃ sthāpitatā /
Vin_13.32 / na naṣṭaprakṛtinā /
Vin_13.33 / nāśīlaikyena /
Vin_13.34 / nānayoḥ /
/ pārikarmaṇavastupṛcchā // 13


________________________________________________


*Vin_14. karmabhedavastu
**(Vin_14,1) karmabhedaḥ
Vin_14.1 // na nānātvāya saṃghasya prabhāviṣṇum akā[58a4]maṃ codayed unmoṭayed vā codayatvaṃ /
Vin_14.2 / na yatra prativirodhas tena sārdham abhinamane samāsīta /
Vin_14.3 / dvitrāsanāntaritam anyatra /
Vin_14.4 / evam itaras tena /
Vin_14.5 / antaritasyānayor vihārasya deyatvaṃ grāhyatā ca /
Vin_14.6 / dharme vinaye caitadvatām adharme ced abhiniveśo jñātvā saṃghasāmagrīn na vidyate /
Vin_14.7 / tasmān na tad anyānāṃ saṃbhūya kṛtau karmaṇo rūḍhin na paraspareṇāvyagratvam* /
Vin_14.8 / [58a5] kaliparāyaṇatva eṣā tadvipakṣasya cāvandyatvam idaṃ dharmabhiḥ /
Vin_14.9 / pratyutthānāsanopanimantraṇāsaṃlapanālapanasaṃmodanavyavalokanālokanānām apy akaraṇaṃ /
Vin_14.10 / lūhaśayanāsanānupradānaṃ hastasaṃvyavahārakena /
Vin_14.11 / vacanenānyatra sasūtam ity aparam* /
Vin_14.12 / pratyante vihārasya /
Vin_14.13 / mṛddhadvā vayam iti vadatsu yūtham api śramaṇāḥ śākyaputriyā sma ity ātmānam* [58a6] pratijānīdhve /
Vin_14.14 / yeṣāṃ cedaṃ vṛttam iyaṃ vārtā kāruṇiko vaḥ śāstā yenaitad anujñātam etad api vo na prāpadyata iti prativadeyur anyatra /
Vin_14.15 / na bhikṣuṇyāsanamokṣaṃ hāpayet* /
Vin_14.16 / dadītopāsakapiṇḍapātam /
Vin_14.17 / nāpi sāritāām eṣāṃ sāmagyasya vinā sāmagrīlābhenotthāpanaṃ /
Vin_14.18 / na vinā poṣadhena prakṛtisthatāprāptiḥ /
Vin_14.19 / datvapinaṃ kuryuḥ /
Vin_14.20 / karmaṇaitat* /
Vin_14.21 / pūrvaṃ ca /
Vin_14.22 / [58b1] kalpate sāmagrīmaṅgalārthamāpadi poṣadhaḥ /
Vin_14.23 / tasyaiva cātra kālasya nimittatvaṃ /
/ karmabhedavastu //

**(Vin_14,2) pṛcchāgataḥ /
Vin_14.24 / karmaṇaḥ kṛtāvadharmavādibhir antaḥsīmni pṛthak tadbhedo tadacittena /
Vin_14.25 / rūḍhir asmin* pratisvaṃ karmaṇaḥ /
Vin_14.26 / nāsvapakṣaṃ prati /
Vin_14.27 / dharmavādi kṛtatā saṃghasya kṛtatvaṃ /
Vin_14.28 / sthalasthair atra sanni ced bhikṣuṇīnām acodyatvaṃ /
Vin_14.29 / vyagratvam eṣāṃ dharmapakṣaiḥ /
Vin_14.30 / dhvanso nuvidhau ta[58b2]ttvasya /
Vin_14.31 / nainaṃ kuryāt* /
Vin_14.32 / acodyatvam* pakṣāparapakṣavyavasthitasya bhikṣuṇīsaṃghasya /
Vin_14.33 / nainaḥ bhinnasya /
Vin_14.34 / samagrya yācamānānāṃ niyojyatvaṃ /
Vin_14.35 / dharmatrādini gāmitvaṃ vārṣikasya /
Vin_14.36 / ubhayasannipāte cāvibhajyāpratipātitasya saṃghe vaibhājyasya /
Vin_14.37 / saṃghaparimāṇatā cet tatra teṣāṃ /
Vin_14.38 / janatā cetir eṣām /
Vin_14.39 / tat tatā yadīyasyotsaṃghe pratipādanaṃ [58b3] dvayoś ced ubhayatra /
Vin_14.40 / pudgalaso rāṃśitvaṃ na saṃghaśaḥ /
/ karmabhedavastugate pṛcchā māṇavike // 14

*Vin_15. cakrabhedavastu /
Vin_15.1 / jñapanato vā pṛthagbhāvasya dharmāt saṃghabhedaḥ /
Vin_15.2 / śalākāgrahaṇato vānenārthena /
Vin_15.3 / arūḍhir asyāsaṃghaparimāṇatve bhidyamānānām asatve cānyeṣām antaḥsīmni saṃghaparisānānām adharmadharmayoḥ tathātvena pratyavagatāv ānantaryaṃ /
Vin_15.4 / dharmasaṃjñi[58b4]no pi bhede /

*Vin_16. adhikaraṇavastu

Vin_16.38 / bahutaramatena saṃsthānam ity aparaḥ saṃpratipādanaprakāraḥ /

Vin_16.41 / kharamarthipratyarthikair gṛhītatve pragāḍham* ca vyāḍhatve teṣāṃ bhedāśaṃkitāyām asya saṃsrayaṇaṃ /
Vin_16.42 / asaṃvaraṇakaraṇīyetve rthasya /

Vin_16.63 / amūḍhavinayasyānte

**(Vin_17,2) paścimaśayanāsanavastu /
**(Vin_17,2,1) vandanam /
Vin_17.81 / sapraṇāmāṃ vacam andhakāravandanasthāne niścārayet* /
Vin_17.82 / lopacāraprāptaprasṛto nyasya vandanena vandet* /
Vin_17.83 / kṛtatvam asya brāhmyāṃ ṣāmīcyam /

Vin_17.85 / na vandamānaṃ nārogyayet* /
Vin_17.86 / nāvandyatvam atītāyātatpratyayāḥ /
Vin_17.87 / na paliguddhaṃ vandet* /
Vin_17.88 / [60b6] na paliguddha caret* /
Vin_17.89 / naināṃ svīkurvīt* /
Vin_17.90 / na paliguddham* /
Vin_17.91 / dvayaṃ paligodho bhakṣyamāṇena vā dantakāṣṭhād aśucinā vā tadbhūmiparikarmaṇāt* /
Vin_17.92 / paligodha tatra nāgnyam ekacīvaratā cadevandane pañcamaṇḍalakena jaṃghaprapī[ḍa]nikayā ca /
Vin_17.93 / na kṣut*vantaṃ jīv[e]ty abhivanded utsṛjyāntyāvayasamāgārikāṃ ca /
Vin_17.94 / navakam enam ārogyayeta /
Vin_17.95 / [61a1] / / vanded vṛddham* /

**(Vin_17,2,2) nāmagotrāgrahaṇam /
Vin_17.96 / kṣutvā ca /
Vin_17.97 / nāyuṣman nāmagotravādena tathāgataṃ samudācaret* /
Vin_17.98 / nāsya nirūpāpadaṃ nāma gotram vā gṛhṇīyāt* /
Vin_17.99 / na vṛddhasya /
Vin_17.100 / pratirūpam atra sthavirāyuṣmator upapadatvam* /
Vin_17.101 / na pūrvatra /

**(Vin_17,2,3) navakarma /
Vin_17.102 / gamanāgamanasaṃpannava[stu]ni navakarmiko vihāraṃ prati sthāpayet* /
Vin_17.103 / vṛkṣavāpīcaṃkramaiḥ /
Vin_17.104 / upavicāreṇa /
Vin_17.105 / avyākīrṇavi[61a2]lāpaśabdanirghoṣe /
Vin_17.106 / kāraṇam anujñāte dātrāvihārakaraṇārthād vastunas tatkaraṇabhāṇḍasya /
Vin_17.107 / layanasyāsya sthāpanāya dānam* /
Vin_17.108 / krayas tadupayojyasya tailādeḥ mātrayā /
Vin_17.109 / bhojanaṃ navakarmakeṇa tādṛśasya yādṛśyaṃ yavane /
Vin_17.110 / nirvihārasya tasya sthānasya /
Vin_17.111 / pragrahaṇaṃ snehalābhasya /
Vin_17.112 / sāmantakavihāre pañca[pu]ratvaṃ vihāreṣu parya[61a3]ntaḥ /
Vin_17.113 / tripuratvaṃ bhikṣuṇīnāṃ /
Vin_17.114 / atirecanaṃ gandhakuṭivātāgrapotikayoḥ puradvayena /
Vin_17.115 / niravadyam eṣāṃ purojitve bharasya purodveṣṭanam* /
Vin_17.116 / prārabdhasya ca vṛhatto lpasya vā karaṇārthaṃ bhañjanam* /
Vin_17.117 / bṛhatvārthaṃ [stū]papratimayoḥ /
Vin_17.118 / sīrṇatānimittaṃ tulyayor api niṣṭhitayoś ca /
Vin_17.119 / pradeśasya ca pratisaṃskaraṇārtham /
Vin_17.120 / avatāraṇañ ca katrādīnāṃ /
Vin_17.121 / anyā[61a4]ropanāyāpi /
Vin_17.122 / naitadartham anuṣṭhāpitā nayet* /
Vin_17.123 / jātakādicitrabuddhavacanalekhanayoś ca /
Vin_17.124 / bhaṃgyasyaiṣa viśeṣasya kriyāyai /
Vin_17.125 / karaṇam akṛtāvārabhyānyena śeṣasya /
Vin_17.126 / deyatvam ardhotthite saṃghārthañ ce[d] utthānakasya /
Vin_17.127 / paścādbhaktaṃ taddāne kālo hemantaś ce[d] grīṣmaś ceti pūrvabhaktaṃ /
Vin_17.128 / bhaktakaraṇīyakālasya śeṣaṇaṃ /

**(Vin_17,2,4) yātrāpravartanam /
Vin_17.129 / nāsajjī[61a5]bhūya tato yatrāyāṃ pravartet* /
Vin_17.130 / prakṣālitaṃ hastapāttatvaṃ tadantaḥ /
Vin_17.131 / purobhaktikam utthānakārakaḥ samādāpayet* /
Vin_17.132 / paścadbhakte pānakahastapādābhyaṃgaṃ /

**(Vin_17,2,5) dvārādikaraṇam /
Vin_17.133 / nayanānāṃ dvārakaraṇaṃ /
Vin_17.134 / kacāṭadānam* /
Vin_17.135 / āyāmakaṭakacarmakhaṇḍikayoḥ /
Vin_17.136 / vātāyanakaraṇam /
Vin_17.137 / madhyebahiḥsaṃvṛtasyābhyantare viśālasya samudrākṛteḥ /
Vin_17.138 / jāli[61a6]kādānam* /
Vin_17.139 / kavāṭikāyāś cakrikāghaṭikāśūcīnāṃ /
Vin_17.140 / ajapādakadaṇḍadhāraṇam* /
Vin_17.141 / arāmathaina vānanaṃ /
Vin_17.142 / karaṇaṃ prāsādasya [vya]yanāgrataḥ /
Vin_17.143 / saptāṣṭeṣṭakāstaradānam* /
Vin_17.144 / taduparinyāsapaṭṭasya /
Vin_17.145 / tasya staṃbhapaṃkteḥ /
Vin_17.146 / teṣāṃ trikaṭapatrāṇāṃ /
Vin_17.147 / teṣāṃ sikānāṃ /
Vin_17.148 / tāsāṃ dharaṇīnāṃ /
Vin_17.149 / tāsāṃ paṭṭānām* /
Vin_17.150 / [61b1] teṣām iṣṭakāstarasya /
Vin_17.151 / tasya kṣodakasya /
Vin_17.152 / aprapātārthaṃ vedikakaraṇaṃ /
Vin_17.153 / akampanāyām asyām avasaṃgadānaṃ /
Vin_17.154 / lohakīlakair asya saṃparvaṇam* /
Vin_17.155 / sopānasyātirohārthaṃ karaṇaṃ /
Vin_17.156 / adhaḥśailamayasya /
Vin_17.157 / mṛnmayasya /
Vin_17.158 / madhye /
Vin_17.159 / upari dārumayasya /
Vin_17.160 / adhirohen niḥśrayaṇyā /
Vin_17.161 / dāruvaṃsa(ṃ)rajjumayyām api /
Vin_17.162 / iṣṭakāstaraṇapu[61b2]ṣkariṇikāyāṃ dvārakoṣṭake cākardamībhāvāya dānam* /
Vin_17.163 / tadupari kṣodakasya /
Vin_17.164 / sudhāyās tasya /
Vin_17.165 / abhāve kāṣṭhapaṭṭasya padatrāṇārtham* /
Vin_17.166 / antare ntare vaiṣṭakāyāḥ /
Vin_17.167 / caitye py etat* /
Vin_17.168 / kṛtatvam asyāvyāmamātre kṛtatāyām /

**(Vin_17,2,6) siṃhāsanādikaraṇam /
Vin_17.169 / si[ṃ]hānasya karaṇañ caturasrakasya /
Vin_17.170 / si[ṃ]hamukhatvaṃ pādakeṣu /
Vin_17.171 / grahaṇāya saṃcāraṇe lohakaṇṭakānāṃ catu[61b3]ṣke py eṣu dānam /
Vin_17.172 / paṭṭikābhiḥ dānam* /
Vin_17.173 / masūkarasyādānam* /
Vin_17.174 / upari vitānasya /
Vin_17.175 / lambanānāṃ sopānakasya karaṇam iṣṭakāmayasya sthire /
Vin_17.176 / saṃcārye kāṣṭhamayasya /
Vin_17.177 / asaṃpattau niḥśrayaṇikāyāḥ /
Vin_17.178 / pādapīṭhasya karaṇam* /
Vin_17.179 / patravaibhaṅgukānām upari dānam* /
Vin_17.180 / kakṣapiṇḍakasya vā /
Vin_17.181 / pādayor ālambanam atrā[61b4]rthaḥ /
Vin_17.182 / saṃpattir asya śilayā kākacaṭakayoḥ /

**(Vin_17,2,7) jālādidānam /
Vin_17.183 / pārāvatebhyo bhuñjānānā[mivi]heṭhāya jāladānam* /
Vin_17.184 / cāturvidhyam asya /
Vin_17.185 / mauñje vāvalvajaḥ sāṇakaḥ kārpyāsikā iti /
Vin_17.186 / cakrikāṇāṃ caturṣu koneṣu dānaṃ /
Vin_17.187 / tāsu bandhaḥ /
Vin_17.188 / sphuṭa(nā)naṃ kledaś ca kāṣṭhasya tasmād ayomayīnāṃ /
Vin_17.189 / chidrasyāsyaikadeśe karaṇam /
Vin_17.190 / bhukte prave[61b5]śāya /
Vin_17.191 / velāyāmasya pidhānam* /
Vin_17.192 / pānīyena prāsādasyāplavanāya varṣāsu paṭṭānāṃ dānaṃ [sta]mbhāntareṣu /
Vin_17.193 / ālokāya pradeśam utsṛjya /
Vin_17.194 / abhāve kiṭakānāṃ kiliñjānām vā /
Vin_17.195 / vārṣikamāsacatuṣṭayānte panayanam* /

**(Vin_17,2,8) maṇḍalavāṭādikaraṇam /
Vin_17.196 / karaṇaṃ maṇḍalavāṭasya /
Vin_17.197 / śītalasthānatāyai bahiḥ bhittidānam* /
Vin_17.198 / stambhapaṃkteḥ /
Vin_17.199 / vā[61b6]tayanamuktiḥ /
Vin_17.200 / āsanottamasamānakakṣyāparimānāntānām* /
Vin_17.201 / jālikākavāṭikayoḥ dānam* /
Vin_17.202 / karaṇabhaktāgnyupasthāpanacaṃkramaṇaśālānām* /
Vin_17.203 / avacchādanakānāñ ca kaṇṭhādeśaparikṣiptānāṃ /

**(Vin_17,2,9) bhūmigṛhakakaraṇam /
Vin_17.204 / kalpate bhūmigṛhakam* /

Vin_17.206 / veṣṭikatvañ ca kanthāyāṃ pravrajitārāmasya /
Vin_17.207 / [62a1] / / muktodakabhramatvañ ca bhitt[e]ḥ /
Vin_17.208 / vāṭaparikhābhyāṃ ca /
Vin_17.209 / pudgalasya ca vihāraḥ saparikaraḥ /
Vin_17.210 / karaṇaṃ nīlādikṛtsnanimittāmukhībhāvāya nīlādicaturvidhyasya layanabhittīnāṃ /

**(Vin_17,2,10)citraṇam ārāmasya /
Vin_17.211 / kalpat[e] citritatvaṃ pravrajitārāmasya /
Vin_17.212 / dvāre yakṣāṇāṃ citraṇaṃ vajradharādihastānāṃ /
Vin_17.213 / dvārakoṣṭhake saṃsāracakrasya /
Vin_17.214 / gaṇḍapañcakasya karaṇaṃ /
Vin_17.215 / ūrdhaṃ d[e]vamanuṣyā[62a2]ṇām /
Vin_17.216 / caturṇāṃ dvīpānāṃ /
Vin_17.217 / aupapādukānāṃ satvānāṃ ghaṭiyaṃtravaccyavamānānām upapadyamānānāṃ ca rāgadveṣamohānāṃ pārāvatabhujaṃgasūkarākāreṇa /
Vin_17.218 / grasyamānayor mohena pūrvayoḥ /
Vin_17.219 / pratītasamutpādasya sāmantake dvādaśāṅgasya /
Vin_17.220 / sarvasyānityatayā gra[sta]sya /
Vin_17.221 / ūrdhaṃ buddhasya śuklaṃ nirvāṇamaṇḍalam upadarśayet* /
Vin_17.222 / gāthayo[62a3]r ārabdham iti dvayor adhastāt* /
Vin_17.223 / ākhyātur asya sthāpanam* /
Vin_17.224 / sāmantakenāsya mahāprātihāryamārabhaṅgayoḥ /
Vin_17.225 / prāsāde jātakānāṃ /
Vin_17.226 / mālādhārāṇāṃ yakṣāṇāṃ gandhakuṭidvāre
Vin_17.227 upasthāpanaśālāyāṃ sthavirapaṃkteḥ /
Vin_17.228 / gan*jadvāre ṅkurahastānāṃ yakṣāṇāṃ /
Vin_17.229 / khādyahastānāṃ bhojanamaṇḍape /
Vin_17.230 / jentākāśālāyām aṅkurakaśahastānāṃ kubhā[62a4]ṇḍānāṃ cāgnidvīpayatāṃ /
Vin_17.231 / agniśālāyāṃ mecakādi kurvatām agniṃ* ca jvālayatāṃ kumbhāṇḍaputrāṇāṃ /
Vin_17.232 / dānapater dīpaṃ dhārayato devadūti yasya ca /
Vin_17.233 / nānālaṃkāravibhūṣitānāṃ kalaśa[hastā]nāṃ nāgakanyakānāṃ codakaṃ dhārayantīnāṃ pānīyamaṇḍape /
Vin_17.234 / glānakalpikaśālāyāṃ tathāgatasya glānam upatiṣṭhataḥ /
Vin_17.235 / varcaḥpra[62a5]srāvakuṭyoḥ śivapathikāyāḥ śiraṣkaroṭer vā /

**(Vin_17,2,11)vihārasammārjanādi /
Vin_17.236 / na vihāre nabhyavakāśe sadhūmam agniṃ* kuryād dhārayed dhārakuṭṭime sarvaṃ /
Vin_17.237 / dhārayet tadarthaṃ bhraṣṭikāṃ /
Vin_17.238 / samāvartanārthañ cāyomayaṃ daṇḍatapakam* /
Vin_17.239 / ḍhiṃ*sukenāpi dārumayenaitatkāryasampattiḥ /
Vin_17.240 / vihāram upadhivārikaḥ saṃmṛ[hyā]t pratyahaṃ /
Vin_17.241 / asaktāv upayujyamānaṃ pradeśaṃ /
Vin_17.242 / avaśiṣṭam aṣṭamyāṃ caturdaśyāṃ ca sarvasaṃghe [62a6] gaṇḍīm ākoṭṭya dharmyayā vā kathayāryeṇa vā tūṣṇīmbhāvena /
Vin_17.243 / dharmotsave sekaḥ sukumāryāś ca gomayakārṣāḥ pradānam* /
Vin_17.244 / snānam antera /
Vin_17.245 / hastapādaprakṣālanam vā /
Vin_17.246 / gātrasya codakadigdhenānuparimārjanam* /
Vin_17.247 / snehalābhasya karaṇaṃ /
Vin_17.248 / ratnārthaṃ saṃmṛṣṭāmṛṣṭayor gandhakūṭipratimācaityayaṣṭichayānāṃ cāryāṃ gāthāṃ paṭhatā laṃghaṇaṃ /
Vin_17.249 / śayanā[62b1]sanasyānayor evāhnoḥ pratyavekṣaṇaṃ saṃskaraṇaṃ niḥsṛtaiḥ /
Vin_17.250 / sekasaṃmārgasukumārigomayakārṣāpradānāni vāsavastuni kurvīt* /
Vin_17.251 / śayanāsanaṃ malinaṃ prasphoṭayet* /
Vin_17.252 / atīva ced dhāvet* /
Vin_17.253 / ūrdhaṃ sekāssaṃsṛṣṭiḥ /
Vin_17.254 / tata[ś] ca prajñapanam(a) /
Vin_17.255 / na prasphoṭite sarajaskatāyām ādhāre /
Vin_17.256 / prajña[pra]nīyebhyo vastrasyaikasya prasphoṭane viniyogaḥ /
Vin_17.257 / lūhasya /
Vin_17.258 / prati[62b2]saṃskaraṇam asya /
Vin_17.259 / aśakyatāyāṃ cīrīkṛtya yaṣṭyām upanibadhya prasphoṭanam* /
Vin_17.260 / tathāpy ayogyatve gomayamṛdāstambhasuśire kuṇyasya vā lepanam* /
Vin_17.261 / puṇyābhivṛddhiciratāyai dāttaḥ /
Vin_17.262 / na dvārakoṣṭhake prāsāde vā śayyāprajñaptiṃ kṛtvā vā dhāraṇaṃ kuryāt* /
Vin_17.263 / kuryād aśadrava pratipakṣeṇārtham aṣṭamīcaturdaśai prāsāde /

**(Vin_17,2,12)maṃcapīṭhādidhāraṇam /

**(Vin_17,2,13)sahāniṣīdanam /
Vin_17.275 / nāpareṇe sārdham ekatra maṃce saṃ[s]tare nyatra vā /
Vin_17.276 / kalpayed asaṃbhave lajjī pṛtha[k] pratyāsthī[tyā]ntare vṛṣikāpātrasthāvikādi dattvā smṛtim upasthāpya /
Vin_17.277 / na trayād ūrdhaṃ pracitiḥ sāhyena maṃcarūḍhatāṃ bhajet* /
Vin_17.278 / na dvayā dhīrghapīṭhi /
Vin_17.279 / nāsaṃtyām anekaḥ /
Vin_17.280 / na trivarṣāḥ pareṇāntaritena sārdham āsanasya /
Vin_17.281 / bhaje[d] āntargṛhe [62b5] upādhyāyenāpy āsanābhāve smṛtim upasthāpya /
Vin_17.282 / na kvacid gṛhiṇānupasaṃ[(n)pa]nnena vā /
Vin_17.283 / na ṣaṇṇadṛpaṇḍakamātṛghātakāditīrthyatīrthyākrāntaka[ste]yasaṃvāsikanānāsaṃvāsikāsaṃvāsikaiḥ /
Vin_17.284 / na śi[kṣā]dattakaḥ /

**(Vin_17,2,14)sāṃghikapariṣkāreṣu vartanam /
Vin_17.285 / śikṣādattakenāsanatvaṃ cilinimikāyāḥ sopasaṃpatsaṃghasannipātād anyatra /
Vin_17.286 / na sthalikāyāḥ saṃkaṭasaṃbādhaprāptā[62b6]v anāpattiḥ /
Vin_17.287 / saṃcāraṇe śayanāsanasya dvau ced ekena maṃcapīṭhasya vā grahaṇam apareṇa vṛśyādeḥ /
Vin_17.288 / naita[tsā]ṃghikamadayam ākarṣenniṣkarṣed dhīna tathā kuryād yathāsya
[drū]mamalarajobhiyogaḥ saṃpadyet* /
Vin_17.289 / nāsyāśucikuṭyoḥ sā[nni]hityam bhajet* /
Vin_17.290 / na vinasya chorayet* /
Vin_17.291 / ātapanaṃ sye śoṣaṇaṃ prasphoṭanaṃ chidrer gaḍakadānam* /
Vin_17.292 / da[ṇḍa]kasya sphoṭo /
Vin_17.293 / [63a1] kṣīṇamadhyasyāntayor madhyatākaraṇam /
Vin_17.294 / raṃjanaṃ tad arhasya /
Vin_17.295 / aśakyapratisaṃskaraṇatāyāṃ dīpeṣu viniyogo vartikātvena ratnopayogeṣu pudgaladātṛkeṣv api /
Vin_17.296 / anupayajyamānasyātra kardamena bhittistambhakavāṭasuṣireṣu ratneṣu lepanam ity anupratipattiḥ /
Vin_17.297 / addeṣṭasye gṛhītrā /
Vin_17.298 / śiṣṭasya saṃgh[e]na saṃnipatya gaṇḍyākoṭanena /
Vin_17.299 / na śa[63a2]kyaṃ sāṃghikam apaharantaṃ dṛṣ[ṭra] na nivārayet* /
Vin_17.300 / no trāse sāṃghikam avyupekṣeran* /
Vin_17.301 / asaṃprāptasya sthānam* /
Vin_17.302 / netarūpatraiyojyatvaṃ /
Vin_17.303 / paribhuktir asaṃbhave svasthānopanayanasya sthānāntare paribhogena /
Vin_17.304 / na sthānāntarīyaṃ bhaktopakaraṇalābhaṃ sthānāntare paribhuñjīt* /
Vin_17.305 / tenamanyasmai dadyuḥ /
Vin_17.306 / dāsyatvaṃ grahītuḥ /
Vin_17.307 / dātur apragame /
Vin_17.308 / nirava[d]yoṃsibhiḥ [63a3] sāṃghikasya svasyaiva nirupayojyasya tṛṇakāṣṭhasyopayogaḥ /
Vin_17.309 / yathāgatikānuddiṣṭa avṛttyopayojyena yathāvṛddhikā /
Vin_17.310 / sāhye yācanasyaiṣāṃ /
Vin_17.311 / nāto viprayuktaṃ viyojayet* /
Vin_17.312 / śuddhatvam udakena pādasyaitat tadbhāvane /
Vin_17.313 / praviṣṭatvaṃ kuṭau tat* /
Vin_17.314 / na niṣadyāyoniṣadyāṣaṇṇam utthāpayeta /
Vin_17.315 / nāsyāṃ yathāvṛddhikā /
Vin_17.316 / na kardamāmiṣapariśuddhaṃ [63a4] bhikṣuṃ /
Vin_17.317 / nāgantryā niṣīdet* /
Vin_17.318 / na saty arthini kṛtakṛtya āvṛddhi bhojyam* dhāray[e]t* /
Vin_17.319 / akṛtakṛtyatvam antarālārthatantratāyāṃ muktāvāsanasya /
Vin_17.320 / cīvareṇainadāyapaṭṭena vā tadādhiṣṭhitaṃ kurvīt* /
Vin_17.321 / nārthisadbhāve satyāṃ gatau sāṃghikasya paliguddhatāṃ bhajet* /
Vin_17.322 / niravadyam evaṃvidhād viyojanaṃ satyarthe /

**(Vin_17,2,15)nāpitabhāṇḍādidhāraṇam /
Vin_17.323 / dhārayet saṃgho niṣadāṃ putrakaṃ cā[63a5]syāḥ /
Vin_17.324 / nāpitabhāṇḍañ ca suktyāṃ prakṣipya bhitto sthāpanam* /
Vin_17.325 / vāsī ca saparaśunakhādanādi ta[d] bhāṇḍam* /
Vin_17.326 / dānam anenāmṛnmayasya bhikṣoḥ yācitakatvena /
Vin_17.327 / na bhikṣuṇīkācabhāṇḍaṃ dhārayet* /
Vin_17.328 / dhārayet sarvaṃ tailabhājanam* /
Vin_17.329 / kaurḍavāt prabhṛtyardhakauḍavāt* /
Vin_17.330 / sthālīmāyasīñ [ca] /
Vin_17.331 / asyāḥ paryaṅkikāṃ /
Vin_17.332 / mṛnmayañ ced dhānam* /
Vin_17.333 / [63a6] labdhasaṃvṛtiḥ daṇḍāṃ /
Vin_17.334 / sikyaṃ caikavarṇaṃ /
Vin_17.335 / da[dyu]r ene? /
Vin_17.336 / jīrṇaglānayoḥ /
Vin_17.337 / saṃbhavaty anayor ekena vacasā dānam* /
Vin_17.338 / dhāraṇaṃ saśabdasya śarīsṛpādipratikriyārthaṃ daṇḍasya /
Vin_17.339 / bandhanaṃ yaṣṭe mūlāsphoṭe kūṭena /
Vin_17.340 / prāntādaṭṭanena /
Vin_17.341 / dhāraye[ccha]traṃ vā rūḍhaṃ [va]rṇamayam vā /
Vin_17.342 / pañjarapramāṇa daṇḍam* /

**(Vin_17,2,16)grāmādicaryā /
Vin_17.343 / nānekagrāmamadhye gaccheta /

Vin_17.346 / nākalpikatvam* /

Vin_17.348 / sthite gṛheṣu sthāpanam* /

**(Vin_17,2,17)āraṇyakakaraṇīyam /

**(Vin_17,2,18)bhikṣuṇyakaraṇīyam /
Vin_17.362 / na bhikṣuṇy araṇye vaset* /

Vin_17.365 / nāvalokanake /
Vin_17.366 / na catuṣpatho /
Vin_17.367 / nāprāvṛtavatī /

Vin_17.369 / nāpidhāyino bāhor gṛhisaṃnidhāne /
Vin_17.370 / ardhaparyaṅko syāḥ paryaṅkasthāne
Vin_17.371 dadīt* prasrāvakaraṇadvāre prāṇakāpraveśāya vastraprabhṛti /

**(Vin_17,2,20)upadhivārakakaraṇīyam /

Vin_17.525 / uttarasya bhaktṛpratipūrvasy[e]ti kalpikasya /
// śayanāsanavastu kṣudrakādigatam* //
// samāptañ ca śayanāsanavastu paścimaṃ // 17 //

Vinayakarmasaṃgrahakārikāḥ
dhāraṇaṃ vipravāsaṃ ca sparśam agner nivārite /
bhojanaṃ bījāghātaṃ ca deśe ca harite śuciḥ //
utsargaṃ vṛkṣārohaś ca śaikṣā u[65a5]ddeśāyos saha /
ratnasparśanabhukyā ca jātas sāṃnidhyānāntayoḥ //
bhūmiprarohaghātābhyām utsṛjyānta ca sūtragataṃ /
pravṛṣe katra vasanaṃ poṣadhas sapravāraṇāḥ //
ityādy asyāntabhāg liṅga yāñcā bhāṇḍopabhugdrava kāmopabhoga saṃvāsānād
arāśodhakavastukam /
sparśapañjaranikṣepau pratichādo nivāraṇam /
trayaṃ kiṃcitkacatuṣṭayaṃ [65a6] gaṇamṛtasīmni ratnataḥ //
chandasaṃmṛṣṭasaṃsparśāc catuṣṭayaṃ bhavati paścimam /
vidhāraṇaṃ saptakaṃ dve cānye dhāraṇādhiṣṭhānoddhārānuddhāra iti //
hiraṇyānyacīvarāsanavarṣakajanasaṃghārthaṃ vacanapalasaṃcataḥ niṣprayojane
hitvānuddhṛto cānuśāṭī ca dvādaśaparṣya nalaṣaṭkaṃ cīvaraṃ
saṃkṣepasyānvananuvyabhiśokabhaṇḍanam /
anvayāśikṣaṇānusthānāt /
[65b1] jatvaṅgulitalaromachannau ca karṇakagrahaṇe bhikṣoś ca vidyāpāṭhanamocana
saṃtagradhāraṇaṃ /
gṛhe channe layane mañce udvarttanamaṃcaka unmuroṭikā gandhapiṇyākataḥ /
snāośīraphalakurvatriśīrṣāṇāṃ kārṇaṅ kāravṛddhādi /
chatropānaha āsandī niṣādārikarttanaṃ coḍā // vikrayagṛhapaticyutvā lasuna
rajādaka dhāvana dānaparivarttanataḥ [65b2] / carṇakulāniṣkāsanantarur dṛṣṭa
sapatha vyathanāvasyaṇḍanakrośānasekāvyupaśayanataḥ /
chandāvavādapoṣadhavarṣaprāvaraṇakaṭhinoddhārabhājanavarṣākā[la?]caryācara-
ṇavādaḥ /
pṛcchā vahiśchoraṇe tiraḥ /
// bhikṣuṇīvibhaṅgoddhānam //
jñapanaṃ sekavākyañ ca satyavākyañ ca tadyathā /
rahontaḥ prasrayor arthapoṣadhasyātra sā yadi //
saṃghe [65b3] vaimatike cāsyāṃ vivādaniṣṭhitatvayoḥ
pravāraṇagate cātra sarvasminn ardhapañcake //
varṣopagamane caiva mṛtārthe prativastunā /
dāne kaṭhinavastrasya duṣṭhulārocane pi ca //
dāne vstrasya gaṇān catuṣke kulasamvṛti /
tatprasrabdhyau kubje ca sonmajje jñaptimātrakaṃ //
mukhasīmadvayāvipravāsonmattapravāraka /
śayyāsanagṛhagāṇāṃ [65b4] kalpabhūmeś ca sanmati //
kaṭhinasya tadāstartturuddhāro syāvasāraṇaṃ /
vihāro deśikādīnāṃ sthalasthavyūḍhanāyakaṃ //
śalākam vārakānāṃ vihārakuṭideśane /
codakasyāpravāsāya sanmetaṣyā tra cāriṇāḥ //
aprasādapravedāvavaditrorvanavedinaḥ /
avandanānalārthaṃ ca daṇḍaśikṣārtham eva ca //
ekalābhakriyāyāñ ca śikṣaṇā na samu[65b5]pasthite /
putre jñātau bahiryāne jñapanaṃ śaikṣyāvāsanaṃ //
upasaṃpādanaṃ tīrthyavāsadānaṃ [ca] mocanaṃ /
sīmnaḥ sāmragra dānaṃ ca poṣadhasya ca saptakaṃ //
ṣaṭkaṃ ca smṛtyasaṃmūḍha tatsvabhāvagamaṣṭakaṃ /
ājñaptadhvastadānaṃ ca jñapanaṃ satrivācanaṃ //
// vinayakarmasaṃgrahakārikāḥ samāptāḥ //
// samāptaṃ vinayasūtram / [65b6] kṛtir ācāryaguṇaprabhasya //
// anena puṇyena sarveṣāṃ lokapiṭakabhājanam //
śākyabhikṣu dharmakīrttinā sattvārthe likhitaṃ śrīmad vikramaśilām āśritya
phālguṇam āse //
gnur chos kyi grags pas bris pa / dpal ldan 'vyri krama śi lar dpye 'sla ra va la
(= gnur dharmakīrttinā śrīmadvikramaśilāyāṃ phālguṇe māse )
pratham mukhapatre (1a)---
śī la a ka ra sa bris pa (= śīlākaraṇe likhitam)
vigrahavyāvartanī pustakānte
gnur dha rma kir tis bris pa jo ca myiṅi mkhan vuyin /
etasya dharmakīrtter vaṇanaṃ debler sro po granthe /
